Welcome to the Civil Rights Annual Training

This mandatory training covers civil rights requirements for USDA food programs TEFAP & CSFP. Please answer the question below to get started.

What is your role?

Your answer determines which training level is required for you.

Please select your role to continue.
🔶 Yellow fields require your input. Fill in all fields, initial each section, and sign both certification boxes. Then click Generate & Save FDU 113 PDF — your completion record (without the PDF file) is synced for administrators, and your completed FDU downloads to this device.

Employee / Volunteer Information

Civil Rights Checklist — Initial Each Section

After reading each section, enter your initials in the yellow box to confirm you have read and understood the material.

Level 1 Training Certification

LEVEL 1 TRAINING CERTIFICATION

I,   (Print your First and Last Name) have read and understood the content of this civil rights training. I agree to follow the civil rights instructions as listed above while working as staff or volunteering for   (Print Agency Name). I understand that this checklist must be reviewed and completed annually.

Level 2 Training Certification

LEVEL 2 TRAINING CERTIFICATION

To be completed by TEFAP and CSFP staff at CDSS, program management staff at any provider (ERA or Local Agency), and lead program volunteers at any distribution site.

I,   (Print your First and Last Name) have viewed and understand the civil rights information contained in the FDU Civil Rights Presentation. I agree to follow the civil rights instructions as indicated in this checklist and in the FDU Civil Rights Presentation while working as staff or volunteering for   (Print Agency Name). I understand that this checklist and the FDU Civil Rights Presentation must be reviewed and completed annually.

CSFP Requirement — Racial & Ethnic Data Collection

Each local agency and/or each sub-site shall collect the number of participants receiving food packages by racial/ethnic category during the month of April each year, unless otherwise specified by CDSS. Self-identification or self-reporting of this information is the preferred method. The FNS-191 report must be submitted each year to CDSS.
